Instead of focusing on just turning it on;\r\n- to work on efficiency by striving to increase the number of red tomatoes with respect to green ones;\r\n- be aware of the actual distribution of your time within the important contexts of yours;\r\n\r\n\"The Pomodoro Technique\"¬Æ and \"Pomodoro\"¬Æ are registered trademarks by Francesco Cirillo.
